## Instruction

You are an investment analysis assistant. Please use Yahoo Finance to perform financial analysis. Create three separate spreadsheets(Note that these are not three sheets in one file) in the designated folder of Google Sheets with the spreadsheet names the same as the sheet names in the excel file `results.xlsx`. Note that I have filled some contents in the excel, for these parts you much copy them without any change and you just need to fill in the rest cells. Please keep 2 decimals for all floating numbers. Cumulative value assumes $10,000 invested at 2020 year-end. Do not include % mark in the cells as we already write in the headers.

c0.542-1.436,1.046-2.889,1.551-4.342c1.037-2.986,2.109-6.074,3.506-8.981c0.39-0.812,1.043-1.897,2.198-1.937l0.165-0.006 l0.136,0.093c0.407,0.281,1.047,0.17,1.666,0.063c1.919-0.332,3.804-0.339,5.664-0.03l0.637,0.105l-0.261,0.59 c-2.812,6.356-5.55,12.845-8.137,19.286l0,0c-0.122,0.302-0.442,0.417-0.673,0.476C36.368,26.439,35.458,26.5,34.458,26.5z l-0.157,0.403c-0.559,1.416-0.991,2.743-0.151,3.425c0.585,0.332,4.794,0.448,5.619,0.162c2.494-6.207,5.128-12.456,7.833-18.587 c-1.542-0.191-3.094-0.154-4.627,0.111C39.084,6.997,38.243,7.142,37.533,6.759z"/></svg> `yahoo-finance get_recommendations`

<Expandable title="Details">
```python

import json

# Historical stock prices
nvda_prices = {
    2020: 13.019115447998047,
    2021: 29.355770111083984,
    2022: 14.600198745727539,
    2023: 49.4971809387207,
    2024: 134.26075744628906
}

aapl_prices = {
    2020: 129.2926025390625,
    2021: 174.09019470214844,
    2022: 128.123046875,
    2023: 190.91366577148438,
    2024: 249.5341796875
}

# Calculate annual returns
def calculate_annual_return(price_current, price_previous):
    return ((price_current - price_previous) / price_previous) * 100

# Sheet 1: Investment Return Comparison
sheet1_data = []
sheet1_data.append(["Year", "NVDA Year-end Price", "AAPL Year-end Price", "NVDA Annual Return (%)", "AAPL Annual Return (%)", "NVDA Cumulative Value ($10,000)", "AAPL Cumulative Value ($10,000)"])

nvda_cumulative = 10000
aapl_cumulative = 10000

for year in [2021, 2022, 2023, 2024]:
    nvda_return = calculate_annual_return(nvda_prices[year], nvda_prices[year-1])
    aapl_return = calculate_annual_return(aapl_prices[year], aapl_prices[year-1])
    
    nvda_cumulative = nvda_cumulative * (1 + nvda_return / 100)
    aapl_cumulative = aapl_cumulative * (1 + aapl_return / 100)
    
    sheet1_data.append([
        year,
        round(nvda_prices[year], 2),
        round(aapl_prices[year], 2),
        round(nvda_return, 2),
        round(aapl_return, 2),
        round(nvda_cumulative, 2),
        round(aapl_cumulative, 2)
    ])

print("Sheet 1 - Investment Return Comparison:")
for row in sheet1_data:
    print(row)
print()

# NVDA Revenue data (in billions)
# From fiscal year ending Jan 2022, 2023, 2024, 2025
nvda_revenue = {
    2022: 26.914,  # FY2022 (ended Jan 2022)
    2023: 26.974,  # FY2023 (ended Jan 2023)
    2024: 60.922,  # FY2024 (ended Jan 2024)
    2025: 130.497  # FY2025 (ended Jan 2025) - this is for 2024 calendar year
}

# AAPL Revenue data (in billions)
# From fiscal year ending Sep 2021, 2022, 2023, 2024
aapl_revenue = {
    2022: 394.328,  # FY2022 (ended Sep 2022)
    2023: 383.285,  # FY2023 (ended Sep 2023)
    2024: 391.035   # FY2024 (ended Sep 2024)
}

# For calendar year mapping:
# 2022 calendar year = FY2022 for both
# 2023 calendar year = FY2023 for both
# 2024 calendar year = FY2024 for AAPL, FY2025 for NVDA

# Sheet 2: Fundamental Analysis
sheet2_data = []
sheet2_data.append(["Year", "NVDA Annual Revenue (Billion USD)", "AAPL Annual Revenue (Billion USD)", "NVDA Year-end P/E", "AAPL Year-end P/E", "NVDA Revenue Growth Rate (%)", "AAPL Revenue Growth Rate (%)"])

# For P/E ratios, we need to calculate based on year-end price and earnings
# NVDA P/E calculations based on trailing EPS at year end
# 2022: Using FY2023 data (ended Jan 2023) - EPS 0.174
# 2023: Using FY2024 data (ended Jan 2024) - EPS 1.19
# 2024: Using FY2025 data (ended Jan 2025) - EPS 2.94

nvda_eps = {
    2022: 0.174,  # FY2023
    2023: 1.19,   # FY2024
    2024: 2.94    # FY2025
}

# AAPL P/E calculations
# 2022: Using FY2022 data (ended Sep 2022) - EPS 6.11
# 2023: Using FY2023 data (ended Sep 2023) - EPS 6.13
# 2024: Using FY2024 data (ended Sep 2024) - EPS 6.08

aapl_eps = {
    2022: 6.11,
    2023: 6.13,
    2024: 6.08
}

for year in [2022, 2023, 2024]:
    if year == 2022:
        nvda_rev = nvda_revenue[2022]
        aapl_rev = aapl_revenue[2022]
        nvda_growth = None
        aapl_growth = None
    elif year == 2023:
        nvda_rev = nvda_revenue[2023]
        aapl_rev = aapl_revenue[2023]
        nvda_growth = ((nvda_revenue[2023] - nvda_revenue[2022]) / nvda_revenue[2022]) * 100
        aapl_growth = ((aapl_revenue[2023] - aapl_revenue[2022]) / aapl_revenue[2022]) * 100
    else:  # 2024
        nvda_rev = nvda_revenue[2025]  # FY2025 for NVDA
        aapl_rev = aapl_revenue[2024]
        nvda_growth = ((nvda_revenue[2025] - nvda_revenue[2024]) / nvda_revenue[2024]) * 100
        aapl_growth = ((aapl_revenue[2024] - aapl_revenue[2023]) / aapl_revenue[2023]) * 100
    
    nvda_pe = nvda_prices[year] / nvda_eps[year]
    aapl_pe = aapl_prices[year] / aapl_eps[year]
    
    sheet2_data.append([
        year,
        round(nvda_rev, 2),
        round(aapl_rev, 2),
        round(nvda_pe, 2),
        round(aapl_pe, 2),
        round(nvda_growth, 2) if nvda_growth is not None else "",
        round(aapl_growth, 2) if aapl_growth is not None else ""
    ])

print("Sheet 2 - Fundamental Analysis:")
for row in sheet2_data:
    print(row)
print()

# Sheet 3: Investment Decision Reference
# Calculate cumulative return from 2021 to 2024
nvda_cumulative_return = ((nvda_prices[2024] - nvda_prices[2020]) / nvda_prices[2020]) * 100
aapl_cumulative_return = ((aapl_prices[2024] - aapl_prices[2020]) / aapl_prices[2020]) * 100

# Calculate CAGR (Compound Annual Growth Rate) from 2021-2024 (3 years)
years = 4
nvda_cagr = (((nvda_prices[2024] / nvda_prices[2020]) ** (1/years)) - 1) * 100
aapl_cagr = (((aapl_prices[2024] / aapl_prices[2020]) ** (1/years)) - 1) * 100

# Current P/E ratios
nvda_current_pe = 52.199432
aapl_current_pe = 38.341946

# Analyst target prices
nvda_target = 218.51369
aapl_target = 248.1203

# Current prices
nvda_current = 183.22
aapl_current = 252.29

# Target price upside
nvda_upside = ((nvda_target - nvda_current) / nvda_current) * 100
aapl_upside = ((aapl_target - aapl_current) / aapl_current) * 100

sheet3_data = []
sheet3_data.append(["Metric", "NVDA Value", "AAPL Value", "Better Stock"])
sheet3_data.append([
    "Cumulative Return (from 21 year end to 24 year end, %)",
    round(nvda_cumulative_return, 2),
    round(aapl_cumulative_return, 2),
    "NVDA" if nvda_cumulative_return > aapl_cumulative_return else "AAPL"
])
sheet3_data.append([
    "Annualized Return (CAGR over 21-24, %)",
    round(nvda_cagr, 2),
    round(aapl_cagr, 2),
    "NVDA" if nvda_cagr > aapl_cagr else "AAPL"
])
sheet3_data.append([
    "Current P/E Ratio",
    round(nvda_current_pe, 2),
    round(aapl_current_pe, 2),
    "AAPL" if aapl_current_pe < nvda_current_pe else "NVDA"  # Lower P/E is better
])
sheet3_data.append([
    "Latest Analyst Target Price",
    round(nvda_target, 2),
    round(aapl_target, 2),
    ""  # No comparison for absolute price
])
sheet3_data.append([
    "Target Price Upside (%)",
    round(nvda_upside, 2),
    round(aapl_upside, 2),
    "NVDA" if nvda_upside > aapl_upside else "AAPL"
])

print("Sheet 3 - Investment Decision Reference:")
for row in sheet3_data:
    print(row)
print()

# Save data for later use
import pickle
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/analysis_data.pkl', 'wb') as f:
    pickle.dump({
        'sheet1': sheet1_data,
        'sheet2': sheet2_data,
        'sheet3': sheet3_data
    }, f)

print("Data saved successfully!")
 code
```

```json arguments
{
```
